    <div><br>

    <div style="text-align: center; font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold;">TOMI ENVIRONMENTAL SOLUTIONS, INC. <font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; color: #000000;">REPORTS
        170% SEQUENTIAL GROWTH IN SECOND QUARTER REVENUE WITH BREAK EVEN EPS</font></div>
    <div><br>
    </div>
    <div style="text-align: center;">-&#160;&#160; Company Reports Operating Income of $122,000 And Positive Net Income&#160;&#160; -</div>
    <div style="text-align: center;">-&#160;&#160; Performance Driven By Growth in International, Mobile Equipment and BIT Solutions Sales&#160;&#160; -</div>
    <div><br>
    </div>
    <div><br>
    </div>
    <div style="text-align: justify; color: #000000; font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 10pt;">FREDERICK, MD, August 1, 2024 &#8212; <font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif;">TOMI Environmental Solutions,
        Inc.</font><sup style="vertical-align: text-top; line-height: 1; font-size: smaller;">&#174;</sup><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif;"> (&#8220;TOMI&#8221;) (NASDAQ: TOMZ), a global company specializing in disinfection and decontamination utilizing its premier Binary Ionization Technology (BIT)
        platform through its SteraMist brand of products, today announced its second quarter 2024 results.</font></div>
    <div><br>
    </div>
    <div style="text-align: justify; font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 10pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; color: #000000;">TOMI Chief Executive Officer, Dr. Halden Shane, stated, &#8220;In
        the second quarter of 2024, we achieved profitability and delivered improved financial results through revitalized revenue growth. These efforts contributed to a quarterly profit of $30,000. Our revenue for the second quarter increased 8.6% year
        over year to $3,000,000, with notable sequential growth of $1,900,000, or 170%, from the first quarter of 2024.&#160; </font>This growth was primarily driven by higher mobile equipment sales, <font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; color: #212529;">a product mix not seen since 2022, with our mobile SteraMist equipment accounting for over 60% of our revenue in the second quarter of 2024</font>.&#8221;</div>
    <div><br>
    </div>
    <div style="text-align: justify; font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 10pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif;">&#8220;We&#8217;re off to strong start in 2024.&#160; For the first time since the end of 2020,
        our outlier year due to the COVID-19 pandemic, we surpassed $3 million in sales. </font>In fact, to date, <font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; color: #212529;">we have nearly matched the total number of
        mobile equipment sales realized throughout the entire calendar year of 2023</font><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif;"> and we remain diligent in our </font>focus on executing our strategies to grow
      revenues, reduce operating expenses, expand business development and deliver improved results and value for our shareholders,&#8221; Dr. Shane concluded.</div>
    <div><br>
    </div>

    <div style="text-align: left; color: #000000; font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold;">TOMI&#8482;&#160;Environmental Solutions, Inc.: Innovating for a safer world&#174;</div>
    <div><br>
    </div>
    <div style="text-align: justify; color: #000000; font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 10pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif;">TOMI&#8482;&#160;Environmental Solutions, Inc. (NASDAQ:TOMZ) is a global
        decontamination and infection prevention company, providing environmental solutions for indoor surface disinfection through the manufacturing, sales and licensing of its premier Binary Ionization Technology&#174;&#160;(BIT&#8482;) platform. Invented under a
        defense grant in association with the Defense Advanced Research Projects Agency (DARPA) of the U.S. Department of Defense, BIT&#8482;&#160;solution utilizes a low percentage Hydrogen Peroxide as its only active ingredient to produce a fog of ionized Hydrogen
        Peroxide (iHP&#8482;). Represented by the SteraMist&#174;&#160;brand of products, iHP&#8482;&#160;produces a germ-killing aerosol that works like a visual non-caustic gas.</font></div>
    <div style="text-align: justify; color: #000000; font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 10pt;">TOMI&#160;products are designed to service a broad spectrum of commercial structures, including, but not limited to, hospitals and medical
      facilities, cruise ships, office buildings, hotel and motel rooms, schools, restaurants, meat and produce processing facilities, military barracks, police and fire departments, and athletic facilities.&#160;TOMI&#160;products and services have also been used
      in single-family homes and multi-unit residences.</div>
    <div><br>
    </div>
    <div style="clear: both; margin-top: 10pt; margin-bottom: 10pt;" class="BRPFPageBreakArea">
      <div style="page-break-after: always;" class="BRPFPageBreak">
        <hr noshade="noshade" style="margin: 4px 0px; width: 100%; border-width: 0; height: 2px; color: #000000; background-color: #000000; clear: both;"></div>
    </div>
    <div style="text-align: justify; color: #000000; font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 10pt;">TOMI&#160;develops training programs and application protocols for its clients and is a member in good standing with The American Biological
      Safety Association, The American Association of Tissue Banks, Association for Professionals in Infection Control and Epidemiology, Society for Healthcare Epidemiology of America, America Seed Trade Association, and The Restoration Industry
      Association.</div>
